I used to clean weekly but switched to daily to help control acne, it worked. However, cleaning solution occasionally lasts only 3-4 weeks, instead of my usual 2 months. What I discovered is that the drain hole back to the reservoir is quite small (to limit evaporation?) but it is so small that it sometimes gets plugged by stubble. Once the hole is plugged the solution gets pumped up to the head cleaing trough but can't drain back so it evaporates very quickly because of the larger exposed surface area.<br /><br />Now I clean out the drain hole every week or two with a cotton swab or toothpick. I also wipe out the crust in the trough with a tissue because it may dislodge and plug the hole. Good solution life since..
